<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tāle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*talō</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">language</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">form of communication consisting of vocabulary and grammar</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">tabaco</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabak.html>tabak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabak.html>tabakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabak.html>tabakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The tobacco plant.</li>

***tabel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a> (42983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tabelle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tabella</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tablet, board, <a href = vnd.unilang:plank.html>plank</a>, chart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally the older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a></i> (which derives ultimately from the same Latin source and thus <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> its doublet) <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> used alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></i> with the same meaning, still seen in the use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a></i> to mean a multiplication table. <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> time, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> differentiated from it.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabellen.html>tabellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabelletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>table (grid of data in rows and <a href = vnd.unilang:columns.html>columns</a>)</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">tabelleren</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">tabulair</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> geordende <a href = vnd.unilang:lijst.html>lijst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegevens.html>gegevens</a>

***tabula.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a> (53098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncertain. Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*th₂-dʰlom</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*teh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (a variety of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i> without s-mobile, whence also Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stō, stāre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*-dʰlom</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instrumental <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> whence Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-bula</i>. The original meaning would then be “that which stands”, for which see also Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stabulum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">tabulae</b>); <i>first declension</i>
</p>
<ol><li>tablet, sometimes a tablet covered with wax for writing</li>
<li>board or <a href = vnd.unilang:plank.html>plank</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> map, painting, document or other item put onto a tablet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">map</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="la">charta</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="la">fōrma</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="la">tabulāria</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">tabulārium</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">tabulātum</span></li></ul>
</body>

***tafel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a> (916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tâfele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tavala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">board</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafels.html>tafels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafelen.html>tafelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafeltje.html>tafeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>table (item of furniture)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">dis</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meal, spread on (a) table(s)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maaltijd.html>maaltijd</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maal.html>maal</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">arithmetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> multiplication table</li>
<li>writing tablet
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tablet</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafelen.html>tafelen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only used in the sense "writing tablet".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tail</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tailback.html>tailback</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tailbacks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A line of <a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> vehicles causing or the result of traffic congestion or a traffic jam; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> backup.
<ul><li><b>2013</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Jenkins, <i>Gibraltar and the Falklands deny the logic of history</i> (in <i>The Guardian</i>, 14 August 2013)<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2013/aug/14/gibraltar-falklands-deny-logic-history">[1]</a>
<dl><dd>The idea of a British warship supposedly menacing Spain <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ludicrous. <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> it meant to bomb Cadiz? Will its <a href = vnd.unilang:guns.html>guns</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a> a rush-hour <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tailback.html>tailback</a></b> in a colony that most Britons regard as awash with tax <a href = vnd.unilang:dodgers.html>dodgers</a>, drug <a href = vnd.unilang:dealers.html>dealers</a> and right-wing whingers? The Gibraltarians have rights, but why British taxpayers should send warships to enforce them, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> if just "on exercise", <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a mystery.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">American football</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A running back or <a href = vnd.unilang:halfback.html>halfback</a> who lines up furthest to the rear in an I formation.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tac.html>tac</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pointy object, forked object</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*takko</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pointy object</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*takkō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*takkô</i>.

***taks.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taks</a> (53091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">taxe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">taxe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">taxa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taks</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taksen.html>taksen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taksje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">tax</span></li>
<li>fee, amount, share</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>Taks</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a common Belgian Dutch word for “tax”. The equivalent term in the Netherlands <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belasting.html>belasting</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taks</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> more limited use there, mostly for brevity and in fixed expressions like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vlaktaks</i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belasting.html>belasting</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffing.html>heffing</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a>)</span> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> dashond <sup id="cite_ref-qtaks2_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-qtaks2-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></li></ol>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:talent.html>talent</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:talent.html>talent</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">talentum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τάλαντον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tálanton</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a particular weight, balance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tl̥h₂ent-</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*telh₂-</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:talent.html>talent</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">gift, quality, capability</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:talisman.html>talisman</a> (18526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:talisman.html>talisman</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طِلَسْم‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭilasm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τέλεσμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">télesma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<ul><li><b>1644</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:johan.html>Johan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Brune, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>Jonge</a>, <i>Wetsteen <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> vernuften</i>, publ. by Iacob Lescaille, page 46.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> d'Arabiers <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:talisman.html>Talisman</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a> Scaliger in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> Fransche <a href = vnd.unilang:brieven.html>brieven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:getuigt.html>getuigt</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> the Arabs give to it the name of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:talisman.html>Talisman</a></b>; like Scaliger attests in his French <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:talmen.html>talmen</a> (62787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:talmen.html>talmen</a></i>, further derivation uncertain. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:talmen.html>talmen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go slowly, tarry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:talmen.html>talmen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to talk aimlessly, to ramble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tálma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hinder, thwart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

***talmud.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> talmud (18759)</h1><br></body> 
***talon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:talon.html>talon</a> (15750)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:talon.html>talon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a>, spur</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:talon.html>talon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:talons.html>talons</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sharp, hooked claw of a bird of prey or other predatory animal.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Francis Bacon to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of certain small prominences on the hind part of the face of an elephant's tooth.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of moulding, concave at the bottom and convex at the top; an ogee. (When the concave part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> at the top, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called an <i>inverted <a href = vnd.unilang:talon.html>talon</a></i>.)</li>
<li>The shoulder of the bolt of a lock on which the key <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> to shoot the bolt.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Knight to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>In various card games, the remaining stock of undealt cards.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:talon.html>talon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tam.html>tam</a> (16945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:tam.html>tam</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tamaz</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>tame, not wild</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boring, unexciting, bland</li></ol>

***tampon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a> (24032)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Nasalized variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tapon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*tappo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tappô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plug, tap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tappen.html>tappe</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zapfen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tæppa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:tampons.html>tampons</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Piece of wood or other material to close an opening.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">…un <a href = vnd.unilang:petit.html>petit</a> orifice qui, pendant l'emplissage, est bouché par un <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bois.html>bois</a>.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ol><li>(musical instrument) Same, closing the opening of a flute, a saxophone.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampons.html>Tampons</a></b> spéciaux montés sur plaques aluminium pour saxophone alto à <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampons.html>tampons</a></b> vissés.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(boat) Same, closing a leak.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>Tampon</a></b> d'étoupe.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A plug of cotton or other absorbent material inserted into a body cavity or wound to absorb fluid.
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1932</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jules.html>Jules</a> Romains,  <cite>Hommes <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bonne.html>bonne</a> volonté</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="fr">Il monta chercher <a href = vnd.unilang:dans.html>dans</a> sa chambre, <a href = vnd.unilang:au.html>au</a> premier étage, un <a href = vnd.unilang:petit.html>petit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b> d'ouate; puis, <a href = vnd.unilang:comme.html>comme</a> le <a href = vnd.unilang:sang.html>sang</a> était sec et collait à la porcelaine, il humecta légèrement le coton avant <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> frotter.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></a> to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> menstruation.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>Tampon</a></b> hygiénique.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sponge, piece of porous material.
<ol><li>used for washing.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b> à récurer.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to varnish or apply wax to a piece of furniture.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernissage.html>vernissage</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:au.html>au</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to apply ink.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>Tampon</a></b> encreur.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li>stamp.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:donner.html>Donner</a> un coup <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mitigator, mediator, buffer between people having a dispute.
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">jouer le rôle <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<ol><li>In this sense, often used in apposition, such as in <i>solution <a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a>, État <a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a>, zone <a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></i>, etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Cette zone accueillerait une partie <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> 3,6 millions <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> réfugiés syriens et ferait office <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> zone <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:avec.html>avec</a> la Syrie.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> buffer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Solution <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Buffer solution</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> buffer</li>
<li>Elastic part that prevents damaging when a collision occurs, e.g. buffer in rail transport.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tand.html>tand</a> (5549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tanþs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃dónts</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tand.html>tand</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tanden.html>tanden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tandje.html>tandje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>natural tooth, more specifically incisor.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebit.html>gebit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaat.html>bestaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tanden.html>tanden</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoektanden.html>hoektanden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kiezen.html>kiezen</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dentition consists of incisors, canines and molars.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>artificial object of similar shape and/or purpose, as on a cartwheel</li></ol>
